<Author>JamieKate
<Content>Not deluxe, but great service There are quite a few hotels around the Marina area in Singapore with not much to distinguish them from each other. The Pan Pacific falls into this category in that there is nothing amazing about it, but I found it a very comfortable hotel. I had a spacious double room with a balcony. The design of the interior is innovative and despite all the rooms being round an atrium there was no noise from the lobby. The rooms are quite bland, but clean and functional. Other plus points of the Pan Pac - extensive room service menu with good quality food, lovely Japanese restaurant in the hotel, friendly helpful staff on reception, at the concierge and taxi rank, comfortable large beds, separate bath and shower, good location for CBD and if you are there on holiday. Downsides - I went to the spa for a massage and was kept waiting for nearly 20 mins, to get to the pool and spa areas you have to go outside, which isn't great if it's raining, spa is not luxurious and definitely overpriced for the setting, which is a bit tatty. If you want beautiful, then like most of the Marina area the surrounds of Pan Pac are v. concrete and look like a multi storey.Overall would definitely stay there again, liked it better than the Shangri La and value for money it beats the Ritz Carlton.

<Author>RobFindlater
<Content>An Excellent Stopover Choice My wife, her mother and our daughter stayed overnight at the Pan Pacific en route back to the UK from Australia.I'd pre-arranged the booking direct with the hotel after initially selecting the accommodation from reading Tripadvisor reviews and then from looking on the hotels web site I noted a good deal if you were flying with Singapore Airlines and signed up to their KrisFlyer programme.Providing certain travel criteria were met and you could show inbound and outbound Signapore airlines boaring passes the deal on offer was a free upgrade to the next available room category, a late check-out and either a limo collection from the airport or a meal subsidy, (we chose the airport collection).Based on my booking experience, which was extremely easy, and my wife's feedback I'd have no hesitation in recommending this establishment. Room - a decent size, great facilities and very clean.Staff - exceptionally friendly and couldn't do enough for my family, especially my baby daughter.Service - fast an efficient.Hotel facilities - excellent, all amenities that my family requested and a very good and clean swimming pool to relax in.Price - I found it offered good value for money based on its star rating, the facilities on offer and location.Location - centrally located, right next to a shopping area if you are after that sort of thing and within 20 mins drive of the airport.Overall - An excellent choice.

<Author>Ninjaman0714
<Content>No complaints Terrific hotel. Room was very clean, great bathroom. Balcony was convenient with a great view over the Marina. Staff were very friendly, and even allowed me a late checkout at no extra cost - and this was on the evening of the start of the F1 Grand Prix weekend, and my room was directly overlooking the circuit. I was very pleasantly surprised that they facilitated me.Staff also attempted to get me linked up with another hotel to check out the Night Safari (as a group, since they themselves did not have any arrangements for that evening). Even though they were not able to find any spot for me for this, this was pretty much my fault, as I only gave them about 3 hours notice. Nevertheless, they made the effort, and when they could not find a group tour for me to join, they gave me full directions and advice on getting it done solo, which I ended up doing, and had a great time.Location is fantastic, connected directly to a few shopping centres. Within Suntec, you can also find a lot of tour companies (close to the food court), such as HiPPO tours (hop on hop off bus tour). Also, within a few minutes walk are the Raffles Hotel (to stop in and have a Singapore Sling), New Asia Bar (71st floor of the Swissotel The Stamford - a must to-do just for 1 drink to take in the view at night). Clarke Quay is also just a few minutes taxi ride away.About 10 mins drive to Little India and Chinatown, Sim Lim Square (great for electronics), 25 mins drive to Sentosa Island, 35-40 minutes to Night Safari. Taxis are easy and affordable, so no big deal.I use the Pan Pacific a lot in Kuala Lumpur, so was pretty confident of the quality when I decided to book this one. No regrets, worth every penny.

<Author>rosietas
<Content>lovely hotel We had a great time at Pan Pacific. Really beautiful hotel and the staff were exceptional. Our room was very nice, well appointed and clean. The only drawback was we were very tired after our flight and went to bed early but couldn't sleep because of the singer in foyer! Never had that problem before! We were given a late check out because our flight was delayed by 8 hours and we were very grateful. A very nice touch and I felt the hotel staff couldn't do enough for us and seem to really care that we were held up.The location is very central and there are numerous shops and restaraunts in the area. Raffles is a short 10 minute walk away but beware if you dine there! We had a glass of house wine each, a peice of fish between us and a serving of fried rice and the bill came to over $125! I kid you not! A once in a lifetime experience!Little India and Arab Street are within walking distance if you like to walk which we do. If you don't you can use the Hop On, Hop Off service outside the hotel. If you fly Singapore Airlines it's free or $12 if not and you can use the ticket all day. It takes you all around the city and is great value. Don't be afraid to travel by public transport as everyone we met were extremely friendly and helpful.So my only real problem with the hotel and I left it until last because I hate to be negative is that before we checked into the hotel and after I paid for the accomodation in advance I sent an email requesting information about doing something special there for our anniversary. No reply and I couldn't help wondering if any one had actually read it! It might not have been important to management but it was to us as it was our 30th wedding anniversary. So one tiny suggestion is that they read emails from their guests.

<Author>TW_Yachtgal
<Content>A great hotel On our recent trip we left the decision on which hotel to book for one night in Singapore to the end as there seemed to be plenty of rooms available. After reading reviews here I had already narrowed our first choices down to five hotels... The Intercontinental, The Fairmont, The Pan Pacific, The Marina Mandarin and the Hyatt. As a one-night stopover we wanted location and luxury for a reasonable charge. In london we booked though Wotif.com.au two days before we were to arrive.. simple, easy. FIRST IMPRESSIONS : Lovely exterior.. extremely friendly welcome from doormen.CHECK IN - no line .. fast, efficient. The best thing of all was that we were asked our departure flight the following day and were offered a 3pm checkout as our plane did not leave until 9pm. ROOMS: The deluxe room was large, modern and impressive with a full bath, and separate enclosed shower and toilets in the marbled bathroom. If we had booked a club room we would have had free WiFi (something all hotels should offer guests for a small one-off fee I think, not outlandish fees as some hotels seem to charge) We needed to check our flight itinerary. The executive level offered Internet acces at a small charge but as we were unable to check in our flight online after a few minutes the fee was waived by the lovely receptionist. ... another big tickEXTRA: a wander to the pool deck revealed a lovely lady named Irene who handed us our towels, a bottle of chilled water and a wonderful smile. Nearby a basket of apples sat next to an array of reading matter ..all conducive to a relaxing afternoon for those who like to relax poolside after a long flight.IN SUMMATION: We were impressed by the staff, the rooms and the hotel in general. We would definitely return to stay here again. Many large city hotels could learn a lot from the way things are done in Singapore.

<Author>Darlox
<Content>Great business hotel near Suntec with a few disappointments The Pan Pacific Singapore is a first-rate hotel in the Suntec City area, connected by skywalks or underground walkways to all of the major venues in this section of town. I stayed here for four nights and found the hotel and its location spectacular, with only a few customer service quirks. Read on for more...LOCATION:The Pan Pacific Singapore is located immediately adjacent to Suntec Convention Center  Suntec City Mall, as well as the Marina Square shopping center. It's in the cluster of hotels that includes the Mandarin Oriental, Conrad and Ritz Carlton. The hotel is about a S$25 taxi ride from the Changi airport, during the late-night hours when most flights to Japan and North America arrive and depart. While the MRT is not easily accessed by this hotel, it's a very simple walk to just about anywhere in the district, and Singapore taxis are extremely inexpensive by most international standards. (The MRT can be accessed by walking through the Marina Square mall, to the One Raffles Link shopping area, then through the underground passage to the City Hall MRT station.)Tourists, be aware: This hotel is definitely situated to be primarily a business property. Unless you plan to take a lot of taxis, you're not really within footsteps of major attractions, or even transit links to reach major attractions. It's a great hotel if you don't mind walking to reach those places, but be aware that you probably will be doing a great deal of walking.ROOMS:The rooms are typical high-class Asian business hotel fare. The sleeping area is spacious with comfortable beds and a work area. The bathrooms are spacious and well-appointed with a large bathtub, a separate shower, and a toilet area with a door separating it from the rest of the bathroom. There is a separate luggage nook and plenty of closet storage. The light switches for the room can all be separately controlled by a bedside console. The rooms all feature full floor-to-ceiling windows (or sliding doors, if you're on the side of the hotel with a balcony), with both sunshade and blackout curtains to control light in the room.AMENITIES:On the Executive Floors, Internet access is included with the room. On the standard floors, Internet is an additional S$25/day, however that is billed in increments of S$0.25/minute up to the maximum, so if you only use a short time on the net, your cost will be less than the daily rate. There are several restaurants offering a variety of International cuisines, an excellent lobby bar with live nightly entertainment, a spa, an in-house tailor, and ample shopping options within steps of the hotel. Given the connection to both Suntec City and Marina Square, literally hundreds of food options are within a 2-5 minute walk of your room -- without even going outside -- if you find that the hotel services are not to your tastes.FRONT DESK / SERVICE:The front-of-house staff are all well-trained and helpful. Luggage service is prompt and friendly. Check-in is reasonably efficient and responsive. However, problem resolution could use a bit of improvement. When I first arrived, the Internet connection in my room was not functioning. After sending an engineer to diagnose, they offered to switch me to a new room the next day. However, the replacement rooms offered were either on lower floors, or did not reflect my room preferences -- or were generally not of the same quality of the room I was leaving, with cause. I would have expected a hotel of this quality to offer a room upgrade for an involuntary relocation, if a room of the same caliber was not available. In the end, we settled on a room in my original class on a lower floor that was acceptable, but still somewhat disappointing to me.ROOM PRICE:Like many business district hotels, the cost of the rooms here seems to be wildly variable. Due to slightly differing check-in dates and length of stay, different people in my same group had rates ranging from S$189/night to as high as S$300/night for a standard room, over mostly the same span of days. Given the high cost of hotel rooms in Singapore in general, I think most visitors will be happy at this property at whatever the best-available price during their stay. Just be aware that substantially better rates may be available for the length of your stay here with only minor tweaking of your arrival/departure.Overall, the Pan Pacific is a great hotel if you'll be doing business in the Suntec or Beach Road areas. I would recommend it to anyone traveling to Singapore.

<Content>Pan Pacific sets the benchmark We booked the Pan Pacific for a short business/ pleasure trip.The price for our booked room seemed very reasonable compared to hotels with similar facilities. We arrived a little earlier than the published check-in time and our room was not ready. However, we were immediately upgraded to a panoramic room which was ready without additional cost. <Author>sailorann
<Content>Fantastic Hotel- A Gem We stayed at the Pan Pacific, Marina Bay hotel in Singapore from October 11th - October 14th. This hotel is right in the heart of the maria square area and is attached to the marina square complex.We arrived at our hotel at 1:30 am due to a delay in UA arrival. The hotel staff was extreamly friendly and warm even at this late check in. We got a great room and our bagged were taken up to our room waiting for us. The room was spectacular! All the ammenities you would expect from a 5+ star hotel. It felt like the spa treatment. The room was comfortable and all international plugs, etc. worked no problem. No adapators needed.The hotel is attached to a huge shopping complex (on of the national passtimes is shopping). We wisely, did not take the package for buffet breakfast as the shopping mall and Suntec city have a variety of places to eat that are substantially lower price than the hotel breakfasts. At night you can also go through Maria Square and get to Glutton Bay. There are a variety of hawkers that set up stalls here where you can sample a variety of local cuisines. Also great for Muslims, as many of the stalls are halal. Take the shuttle bus from the airport it only costs $8 SG per person. You cannot book the shuttle bus back from the hotel, but you can take a taxi. It costs around $21 SG for two people, so a few more dollars than the shuttle bus. If you really want to save a few dollars, then you can go to the Mandarin Hotel also attached to Mariana square, and you can book the shuttle bus from there.Would recommend you also get the tourist card at this mall, it's free and saves you money at a lot of the establishments within the mall. We saved quite a bit of money here!The downside of the location of this hotel is it is a good 10- 15 minute walk to the closest MRT station City Hall. You can walk underground all from the hotel, but it is a bit of a distance.Overall, I loved this hotel. The hotel was beautiful and modern, and the room was fantatic. The staff went out of their way to help us out and answer our questions. They attended to our every need with a smile. I would definely stay here again. Loved it!

<Author>jjstives
<Content>First class, with a few glitches Review for Pan Pacific Hotel, Singapore By almost any standard, this is a first rate hotel. It sits in the fast-paced Market Square area of the city and is close to several great shopping mall complexes and the waterfront. It is not in the more crowded and hustling 鈥渄owntown鈥?area where many other hotels like Marriott, Hyatt, Four Seasons, Hilton and Goodwood are located. The nearest subway station is a good walk from the underground lobby of the hotel. The four night stay was booked through Bookings.com and prepaid. I had a room on the 30th floor that had no great view, looking out on the fa莽ade of the Conrad Hotel next door...not the best view and certainly, as it turned out, not the quietest. Before criticizing, I must point out that Singapore, its hotels and its airline in particular, currently seem to be the most hospitable in the world. From the time I boarded SIA flight 0001 in San Francisco, the courtesy, customer service and facilities exceeded anything I have seen elsewhere in many years. I would compare the hospitality and interest in guests鈥?and visitors鈥?comfort and welfare in Singapore to that of Bermuda in that those people in tourism related businesses seem to understand that service is the key to tourist good will and return business. I must also point out that I picked a very busy and special event week for my visit, even though I did not know this until I got there. It was thus an unhappy turn of events when, on my last night there, the party noise from outside the hotel was such that sleeping in my room was impossible. The volume of what some might call 鈥渕usic鈥?and drumming that would overwhelm the most intense Koto Japanese Drum performance was unending, even for me with less than perfect hearing.  The racket started at around 9PM and went on until after two in the morning. Several calls to the front desk yielded apologies but also the response that there was nothing they could do about it. Unable to sleep, I got dressed and went to lobby and the front desk where a serious, but affable night manager told me there was little they could do because the music was not coming from the hotel but from somewhere nearby.  It was, according to him, a party for the drivers of the Formula One competition that was being held in the city that weekend. If in fact the Gran Prix Race car drivers were partying after 2AM on the day they were to take qualifying rounds on the city鈥檚 newly build racecourse, it seemed unlikely that they would be doing much driving that day.  In any case, the manager told me that even the police could not stop it and moved me to another room for the rest of the night. But my sleep cycle was ruined and I left for Hong Kong the next morning, hardly refreshed and having paid over $900 for the noisy room.  Singapore has some of the strongest laws and law enforcement in the world. Penalties for even small infractions are strict and harsh, so it seemed odd that in this climate the city could not deal with such a disturbance. While it can be argued that this was an abnormal situation, I found it unacceptable at any price and the hotel had nearly tripled its usual rates for this event week. I think that when they do this, they owe a great deal more to the paying guest in terms of meeting normal expectations and common needs, such as a quiet night鈥檚 sleep. My trip had nothing to do with the F1, but everything in the city that week was calibrated towards it, so heaven help the poor soul who, like me, just happened to be there then.  The hotel offered no compensation, only apologies. Not enough for the ruined four day visit and certainly not enough to have me recommend the hotel again.

<Author>Harvsman
<Content>The hotel to stay in, In Singapore!!!! This was the last leg of my trip back to Australia from Europe and Dubai (Emirates are a fantastic airline by the way) I had decided to have a 5 day 4 night stopover in Singapore and had originally booked the Fairmont. However when i saw that the Pan Pacific was nearly $400 cheaper and getting better reviews i cancelled the Fairmont and booked here, best decision i ever made!!!!!!Upon arrival i noticed they have dedicated lines for Arrivals/Departures/Concierge etc, What a great idea i thought! The guy that checked me in was very polite and efficient, Before i knew it i was heading up the glass elevator/lift to my room on the 18th floor. The Atrium is amazing and about 40 stories high. Once i got into the room i noticed it had a bit of a Polynesian theme to it, As does most of the hotel. Truth be told the room itself is probably more of a 4 star but it's the facilities and staff that make this a 5 star hotel. The bed was very comfortable and the plasma tv had about 25 channels including Star World, Star Movies, Mtv etc etc. My room had a nice view of the Suntec Convention Centre and the Conrad Hotel. My room also had electronic blinds but didnt have a balcony, Apparently some rooms do, Some dont. I had a shower and bath, with decent tolietries in the bathroom. I also had a Clock with built in Alarm, etc. I didnt get to use the bar but i noticed each night they had live entertainment with a woman singing. The pool is fantastic and open until 11pm each night! I had a few swims in it and loved the fact they pump music under the water, Great to just lie on your back and look up at the sky! The deep end must of been at least 3 to 4 metres. it was so deep i could never touch the bottom, And i'm 177cm tall so it must be very deep!I never got to use the gym but i did use the business centre, The Internet was very good and the staff up there are so polite and friendly!The location: Probably the only downside but not enough to keep me away. About a 15 - 20 min walk through Citylink, Suntec City and Marina Square mall's. I'd suggest you don't take the MRT from the airport to City Hall MRT and walk to this hotel unless you know the area, Otherwise you could be walking for hours! It is signposted but you've got to know where to look, (If you see a HMV and an American Diner you're heading in the right direction) I'd suggest taking the MRT too the airport on checkout, As by then you should know the area!Staff were very friendly and nothing was too much trouble!If this is an indication of how all Pan Pacific's are i will be making sure i stay in quite a few!Will definitely stay here again next time i'm in Singapore!

The room was spacious, clean, with a great bed and a large balcony with a lovely view of the Fullerton and down-town Singapore. The swimming pool and tennis courts very nice. All in all a great place to stay and one that I'll be going back to.

<Author>charliechunk
<Content>First-class hotel Myself and my hubby stayed at this hotel for 2 nights on the way to Bali for our honeymoon. We were very impressed when we walked into the hotel lobby as its very large and has marble flooring, and a lovely large bar in the centre. Check-in was done in super-quick time. The staff are tremendously efficient and very friendly too. We were upgraded to a room with a balcony and being on the 29th floor, we had an amazing view. The glass elevators on the outside of the hotel are very impressive, if a little bit scary the first time you get in them. Its worth taking the elevator right to the top where the restaraunt is, even if you dont eat there, as its on the 37/38th floor (I think!) and the views over the city are spectaculor. Our room was really nice, however we had twin beds and not a double, but we pushed them together and they didnt seperate at night so there was no falling down the crack incidents! It really wasnt a major problem as we were only there for two nights. The bathroom was lovely too. It was quite big and had a really nice massage shower which we enjoyed very much. We didnt eat in the hotel as we ate out on both nights, but the menu did look nice with a variety of dishes. On our second day, after being shopping, we came back to the hotel to find a huge bunch of gorgeous lillies, a massive fruit basket and a chocolate cake with 'congratulations' iced onto it, which was really really yummy! The hotel is conveniently located and is attached to a shopping mall (one of many) which takes you to the MRT and then its a just a short ride away to the different parts of the city. We got a tourist day card for about $8 sd, which we felt was really good value. Be aware that you will be fined if you are caught eating, drinking or smoking on the MRT. It may seem a bit harsh but when you look at how clean everything is you can understand why they do it. All in all the hotel was a brilliant start to our honeymoon and we'd definately recommend it.

<Author>marxusboy
<Content>A great hotel experience! Stayed at the Pan Pacific Singapore in early August under the Singapore Airlines Boarding Pass Program. Got a good deal that included room upgrade, late checkout and SGD60 food and beverage credit per day. Check-in was efficient and painless, and we were given one of the standard rooms with balcony. We had a great view of the Mandarin Oriental, with the ferris wheel on our left and the merlion on our right. The room was quite nice, with a comfortable but firm king bed, and neat electric blinds with remote control! The only disappointment about the room was the toiletries: their soap and shampoo are, well鈥?extra soapy! I mean, no refinement, no enticing smell or feature, just your standard cheap soapy smells. I like a special treat at shower time when I鈥檓 staying over at a 4 or 5 star property, and it wasn鈥檛 the case here.The pool area is large, with lots of shade and excellent water and towel service. The pool itself is really nice, with the large half on the shallow side and the smaller half quite deep. The gym is also quite large and well set-up; it is actually busier than the pool for some strange reason鈥?br/>Internet in the rooms costs SGD0.25 per minute, capped at SGD25 per 24 hour period, which I found quite reasonable, especially if you plan to do limited surfing during your stay. Breakfast is expensive (the buffet costs SGD35!) and uninspiring 鈥?I think you鈥檙e better off heading to one of the food courts at Marina Place or Suntec City Mall for food (both easily accessible from the hotel through a covered walkway). Their Japanese restaurant is ultra fancy with prices to match (SGD15 for a tiny serving of edamame 鈥?please!)One of the nicest things about the Pan Pacific is their staff; they go beyond the call of duty and are always ultra gracious and helpful. We thought that, all in all, aside from the food quality and prices, this hotel makes for a very enjoyable stay at a very reasonable price. Try getting the Singapore Airlines deal and make it even more worth it!

<Author>Janarella
<Content>Well,, we had a great time!!! Researching our annual Mum and daughters holiday is as rewarding as the actual trip and it is a real bonus when everything falls into place - Pan Pacific gave us a great welcome - We were on the 32nd floor (Panoramic view) facing the harbour. The fruit bowl and mazipan were greatly appreciated. It was also my birthday on the 2nd day and it was a nice surprise to find a yummy birthday cake waiting for us after a day of shopping. There was suficient room for the 3 of us - the balcony gave us extra space - the bathroom was a good size - with bath and separate shower. I slept like a log everynight so I didn't have any problems with the beds - I was up most mornings at the gym - they have a great gym with friendly instructors. I am a bit greedy and like to have the gym to myself - 6.30 to 8.30 it can be a little busy but after this time it is fine. I am not an air conditioner fan - I would sneakily turn it off at night but my youngest daughter complained.Singapore was practising for their National Day so this was another bonus - watching air and water displays, fireworks and what we couldnt see was on a big screen.If you like shopping this is the place for you - right next to the Suntec Centre. Also the Convention Centre that was holding the Singapore Garden Show (if you like orchids like I do it shouldn't be missed)We also tried the Chinese restaurant on the top floor but we weren't too fussed with it - I think we needed a lesson on how to order food but did enjoy the bar on the ground floor - It was pleasant sitting with nibbles and a glass of wine people watching - But anyway we had a great time - We loved the Pan Pacific - bit pricey but what the heck. (We were there for 9 nights)

<Author>Fozzy279
<Content>Pan Pacific - great for business... My experince of this hotel is that while it is very nice, it is very much business orientated with prices to reflect someone else footing the bill. We were on our honeymoon and received a room upgrade to a panoramic view overlooking part of the city. The room had all the ammenities you would expect from a 5 star hotel, and some I'd never seen before - such as a sliding panel allowing you to connect a laptop/USB etc to the large LCD TV - along with a comprehensive set of video/audio leads to hook up your MP3 player to the in room speaker/TV system - a nice touch, but again shows the empasis towards business users. Another nice gadget was the remote controlled blinds/curtains. The 28th floor where our room was was reached by external capsule lifts. I don't suffer from vertigo but felt myself hanging on a few times!!. The hotel is part of a shopping/hotel complex. I felt the shops were all more expensive than home (UK) and was very much geared to the Japanese shopper. This whole complex was expensive proably due to its trendy shops, boutiques and eating places - there are much cheaper places to eat and drink....I felt the food and drinks at the hotel were outrageously priced - especially for holiday makers - again, if a business is paying its not such a problem - a point I made on my customer satisfaction form. I was informed they were competitive with other hotels in the area - but as I later found not competitive with hotels in less trendy areas. As a result, the bars and restaurants were never full and only sparsley filled with busniess people on phones  laptops and as such didn't have a very socialble or relaxing atmosphere. By going to Boat or Clarke Quay - about 10 mins cheap taxi - there are plenty or bars  restaurants offering large discounts and freebies to get you into their establishment - all have a great atmosphere and are very reasonable considering the expensive drinks in Singapore. When I asked the concierge if there were any good places to eat - he didn't know or didn't want to tell - as he wasn't very helpful. Overall, nice hotel, but wouldn't rush back but ideal for business users. Facilities too expensive for holidays if you are on a budget.  
<Date>Jul 24, 2008

<Author>MeInPerth
<Content>Ok, but I expected more for a "five star hotel" I've been to Singapore now a couple of times and tried out five different hotels so far, not only for bargain reasons, but also to be able to compare things. Location: The Pan Pacific is perfectly located to go on an extended Shopping trip as SunTech City and Marina Square are both next door. However the MRT station (City Hall) is still a good five minute walk away, if you want to go to other places.Hotel: The hotel is nice, but for a five star hotel I expected more. The friendliness of the staff has been average. I missed an explanation of the basic things, such as breakfast, Internet access, pool and so on - Nothing! Certainly I could have asked, but I guess customers would appreciate it to get a short overview.The room has been nice, but the level of cleanliness should be improved. During my whole stay the mirrors and the shower haven't been 100% clean as you would expect it from a 5 star accomodation. On my date of departure I could see why, because the room maid thought I had already left. She rushed through the room and used my old towels to clean the shower cabin.The hotel pool is quite nice. I didn't use any restaurant, so I can't review these. Checkout was efficient and correct. Returning home, I realized that I forgot two pairs of trousers in a wardrobe in the room. I used the e-mail function of the hotel's website to contact them; after one week I haven't got any response yet.In general, ok for a 3 or maybe a 4 star, but not for a 5 star. There are less expensive hotels in Singapore which provide the same or even a better service.Maybe the hotel shouldn't sell its rooms cheap on the web. A better way would certainly be to improve the quality. I'm sure customers would spread the word-of-mouth then and help the hotel to fill its rooms.

<Author>Vardomannen
<Content>Good Value for Money I have lost count of the number of times I have visited Singapore - lets face it, if you like food, this is the place to be! I have to admit that when I choose a hotel in Singapore, I often let the price decide, because the quality of all of the hotels I have stayed in here has been excellent. I reserved a deluxe room at the Pan Pacific for two nights, paid around 290 Singapore dollars for the experience and have no complaints. I felt looked after from the moment I arrived ( which included an in-room check-in) until I left (a 30-second check-out). The room was comfortable, well-furnished. The position of the hotel itself is great if you want to be in the colonial district; there are several large shopping centres on the doorstep, loads of restaurants and food courts (don't overlook Singaporean foodcourts - they are really excellent and totally spotless). I got what I paid for ...and then some.

<Author>QP
<Content>Perfect for business travel; also great for leisure stay I stayed at Pan Paicific for 6 nights on a business trip. The hotel stay is by far my best lodging experience while traveling for work!Location - right in the center of the pricy colonial district. It's great for both business/leisure. It's got indoor walkway through a shopping mall to suntec center, so you won't even be exposed to the tropical humidity. Orchard Road (for shopping, not that there's not enough shopping within walking distance of the hotel), is only a brief bus/subway/cab ride away.Room - tastefully decorated in neutral tone. Bathroom has separate shower/bath. Bath tub is generously sized, I used it every night. The room has central light control, very much like any 4+ star hotel rooms in Asia (Japan, HK, Taiwan). Nice audio/visual capabilities w/ the flat screen TV and wireless internet ready. Food - I had room service about 4 times during my stay for both breakfast and dinner. The eggs benedict is one of the best I've had. Didn't have a chance to try the restaurants, but I dare say they probably measure up to the rest of the hotel services well. Amenities - large outdoor pool, which never got busy during my stay there (I had a direct view of the pool from my room). Service - extremely efficient front desk and concierge, no compliants whatsoever!Overall, I just wish that the 5 star hotels in the US could be as nice as Pan Pacific! Tips - Singapore is such an easy country to travel to. There's great shopping and food all around town. Many travel books suggest a day trip to the Sentosa Island. I did just that. However, I don't recommend at all, unless you've kids (even then, there are better attractions on the mainland). The island is full of man made attractions. I was not impressed with anything at all. You'd be disappointed if you're a nature lover or want a taste of the south east asia.

<Author>soulsease
<Content>First Class hotel in Singapore Arriving in Singapore is a great experience; flying in over thousands of ships in the bay, and landing at what looks like a floating city is a great way to arrive! The drive to the hotel from Changi airport is a pleasant 30 minuts or so, along tree lined boulevards. The hotel is located in the business district, near the new Singapore Flyer big wheel (same size as the London Eye, but mounted on a slightly higher plinth, making it the tallest in the world...at the moment!). To get to Orchard Road and the main shopping area is a taxi ride, but the Marina Square mall adjoins the hotel, so if you need to shop, it's all close. You are also around ten minutes walk from Raffles, about 15 mins walk to the main government buildings, 15 mins from the Merlion, and a short cab ride/30 min walk from Boat Key and Clarke Key. The hotel lobby is very well presented; plenty of helpful staff and a stunning atrium bar in the middle. Rooms are large and comfortable, and there is a good selection of restaurants. Try the rooftop Chinese restaurant - food is good; views are stunning! The outdoor glass lifts are also part of the experience!There is a spa onsite, as well as the usual business facilities. The pool area is tastefully laid out, and as soon as you arrive, the staff will present you with a complimentary ice-cold bottle of water, and even better, when you've finished each one, they'll bring you another! Good sized pool as well. Not the cheapest hotel by any means, but well worth it.

<Author>HotelGuru9
<Content>2 Star Hotel with a 5 Star Facade The Pan Pacific is a hotel that looks 4 star, but provided me with 2 star quality service, at very high prices. I suggest you sort the reviews by Lowest First if you want an honest look at this Hotels Reviews. During check in, the man at the counter actually tries to barter with me. He begins a whole act right in front of me, telling me that I had reserved a smaller, cheaper Twin room, for the same $200 rate. I disputed this, and he tells me that I am mistaken. He takes it a step further and lies to me, saying there are no King rooms available anyways. Then an awkward silence, conveying that his decision was final. Astonished by this, and fully aware of what he was doing, I pulled out my reservation and showed it to him. King room with a view. Visibly annoyed he mysteriously finds me my King room with a view 10 seconds later.  Not to be deterred, he then tries to upsell me. Sir, for $90 more per day, you can have free internet and breakfast. I replied I am already paying $200 a night for this room. You basically just lied to me about my reservation so I'd take a cheaper room at the same cost. Internet should be free, and I dont eat $90 worth of breakfast every day. He continued to try and persuade me. He would not take no for an answer. It was very uncomfortable and awkward for me. I felt like I was in a flea market trying to haggle for a bead necklace with a hippie.  Then something surreal happened. He actually has the audacity to inform me - like its the first time he's said it - that he is giving me a Twin room. I started laughing. Seriously? He actually was hoping I had forgotten?? Unfortunately, this theme continued throughout my stay.  The light bulb was out in my bathroom. The grout along the tiles was messy, and smeared. The toilet doesn't flush unless you pump it a few times. When I turned on the sink water, the handle moaned as if it were old metal. The magnet holding the door open doesn't work, so I watched the bellhop try 5 times to make it stick, unsuccessfully. Internet is $30 per day. Absolutely ridiculous. If you go up to the Business Center they actually charge $7.50 for 15 minutes of internet use. I mentioned this to a group of Indian fellows in Little India at an internet cafe, and they responded with roaring laughter. Laundry service here is $10 per shirt. Yes, per shirt. That works out to about $200 USD for an average load of laundry. I opted for their outside laundry service, paid $45 for one load (ugh) and my clothes came back wet. I couldn't make this stuff up, folks...On a Sunday night, I walked outside to get a cab and get some dinner. I ended up standing there for 40 minutes. Yes.... 40 minutes ... in a line with 30 other people, and it was 97 degrees outside. Fully drenched in sweat, I went back in to the hotel to the concierge and said Are you aware that there are 30 people standing in line for a taxi outside? He apologized and started calling to have taxi's come by. I should point out there were six employees standing out there with us the whole time, doing absolutely nothing. The day I checked out, I had overslept and was late for my flight. I conveyed this to the concierge and meekly asked for a taxi as soon as possible. As I stood outside, I watched the hotel staff fill up 6 metered taxis with people from the Taxi line, while I stood there, without a ride. Turns out they had called the more expensive taxi, which I did not want or need. It costs twice as much, and took 10 minutes longer to arrive. Great idea guys! Make that money!!! To top off this already disappointing stay, the more expensive, late taxi driver dropped me off at the wrong terminal. He knew what airline I was taking, yet despite the mercedes and double-fee, he apparently didn't know his job well enough. Remember, I was late for my flight. He takes off, and I had to pay another taxi driver to take me where I needed to go.There are a lot of exceptionally shining 5 star reviews on this hotel, here on TripAdvisor. To the tune of literally hundreds. Way more than one might think is normal. Way more than the other hotels in the same area of Singapore, even right next door. Its interesting to see that the hotel's PR firm heavily involved in responding to reviews here, too. That is something I don't normally see. I can promise that this review was written by a real traveler.

<Author>Montrealais
<Content>Spectacular execution, but a bit boring As other reviewers have said, the architecture is impressive and the service is second to none. I can't imagine anything ever going *wrong* with a stay in this hotel. The only problem is that there's nothing at all to remind you that you are in Singapore, or even in Asia. Very plush, very comfortable, very impersonal. It's in the middle of the convention area, with a view of other hotels and convention buildings.Bottom line: If you need to be close to the convention centre, or thrill in the faultless execution of the hotelier's art, come here. If you want to wake up knowing you're in Singapore, go elsewhere. Cabs plentiful but taking the MRT requires a hike through the shopping centre and underground.

<Author>clanchiefScotland
<Content>Fabulous Pan Pacific We stayed here for 5 nights in January and February on our journey to and from Oz. I could not fault this hotel on anything.The location is great sitting on top of the Marina Square complex which is excellent for dining and shopping. A short walk and you are at the MRT and City link centre. Walk in the other direction and you are at the Suntec Centre.The staff are fantastic. Extremely polite, friendly and helpful. Stop for a moment and someone is sure to approach you and ask if they can help. Check in and out was fast and efficient. Walk outside for a taxi and one was summoned. The rooms, as was the rest of the hotel , are maintained in immaculate state. I loved the large LCD TV tastefully wall mounted and all the sports channels. Almost all the entire outside wall is glass and you can lie in bed and operate(play with) the remote which mechanically brings down the window screen and then a Roman Blind.The views from the room over the city and river were also spectacular. Worth mentioning is the pool and sun bathing area which was great. Very spacious and I spent more time here than any other hotel pool in Singapore. In the heat of the afternoon staff come around with cool towels ,fruit and free bottles of ice cool water. Free water is also provided in the room.The only thing I found missing from the hotel which could inhibit long term tourist travellers from booking was the lack of a guest laundry.Although some may find it expensive the top floor Cantonese restaurant is worth a visit for something special. Although I did not use all of the dining options other guests recommended them and there was a good price spread over these.All in all if I could put this hotel in my case I would and take it to all my destinations around the world.

<Author>Mandelbrot
<Content>Set in a concrete jungle Big, corporate hotel set in a horrible concrete jungle that is Marina Bay. The hotel itself is fine, just as you might expect from a major establishment. Service excellent, restaurants OK, lobby is startlingly garish and over the top. Buffet breakfast was generaly good, and the outside coffee shop by the pool was good(ish) value and OK.Big problem is location. If you want to walk, it takes forever to get to the Metro or anywhere nice, and you have to find your way through a labyrinth of overhead and underground passageways. Unhelpfully, the hotel does not provide a map to guide you, and it took us two days to find the optimum route, by trial and error. It's really designed for people travelling by taxi or car, frankly.I have nothing against this place, but if you are a serious tourist wanting to find your way round the city, I'd find somewhere closer to a metro station and more accesible by foot. Maybe something in Orchard Road, or if you can find the money, the Fullerton looks really splendid and is in a superb location.

<Content>Beautiful Pan Pacific Singapore We delightfully stayed at the beautiful Pan Pacific hotel (Panoramic room) 4 nights for our Christmas Holiday.From the moment we entered the hotel on Xmas day, we were kindly welcomed and immediately directed to check-in desk. Check-in officer recorded passport details. Registration was completed in a kind  efficient manner (took few minutes not long at all). Our bags were brought up promptly by helpful staff to our room on time.Bubble lifts (matrix space-age looking): Clean glass with user-friendly lit buttons. The speed of lifts were appropriate to observe the atrium and amazing views of the hotel鈥檚 interior. In the lifts on our 3rd day, a staff member kindly greeted us and pronounced our surnames correctly. Very polite and accurate! Panoramic Room: Looked brilliant and felt luxurious to stay in. Clean, neat  spacious. Fitted bedding for 3. Plenty of room for 3 large suitcases and shopping bags (which grew larger with each mall visited). Room nicely furnished. Electronic blinds, shades and LCD TV were easy to use. Air-conditioner worked well to our temperature liking. Received free bottles of water each morning plus newspapers. Slippers and robes were also supplied. Mini bar was stocked with goodies (extra charges for eg bottled water from mini bar $4 SGD) and there was also room to store our chocolates in the mini bar. Room was on level 18 and we did not experience any distractions/loud noise. This room had a balcony with beautiful views of Singapore City (Esplanade, Merlion and Marina Bay). Bathroom: Immaculate, neat and polished. Fluffy towels, well-positioned mirrors and nicely accessorised with cute little bottles of shampoos, conditioners, bath gels and bath salts. Hair dryer was handy.Beds: Clean, comfortable and spotless white sheets and pillows. We all slept peacefully well.Swimming Pool: We were busy shopping and left little time to swim at the pool. Nonetheless, on our last night there, we did relax on the seats next to pool and observed the beautiful mini garden scene. Hotel: Magnificent! Check-in and check-out was completed by courteous and polite staff. Check out was prompt and there were no delays to our next destination. Before leaving the hotel room, I had postcards to send back home and staff also helped mail this out within a telephone call. Excellent customer service! Concierge staff were excellent too for taking our luggage out the entrance while we shortly waited there for our driver to pick us up. The door man kindly took a photo for us. Hotel staff are approachable and willing to help. All staff greeted and smiled at us gracefully throughout our stay.Location: Easy access (by taxi or walk) to Marina Square Mall, Suntec City and Esplanade Theatre. Taxi to Orchard Road (5 minutes around $7). Taxi to Sentosa Island around 12-15 minutes (depending on traffic flow).Buffet breakfast @ The Global Kitchen:Delicious and nicely presented food from both Western and Eastern cultures. Courteous staff. Food ranged from prawn dumplings, grilled fish, smoked salmon, stir-fried noodles, scrambled eggs, toast, has browns, mini muffins, dragon fruit, melons, yoghurt, jelly and much more ($35 SGD).Thank you note: ( we have not included our feedback comments on the hotel's online form, instead we will write it here).It was our great pleasure to stay at Pan Pacific Singapore. We are highly impressed and have already recommended this hotel to our family and friends after returning to Australia. We kindly thank all staff for working enthusiastically and kindly servicing us during our holiday period. We have left Singapore but we have not forgotten the pleasant memories of our stay there. All the best to you and we wish you more success and prosperity.

<Content>Pan Pacific Singapore is fab We stayed at this hotel en route to Oz, i have a 5 year old child. the cleanliness and service are impeccable. this is not the hotel in orchard road, but the one next to the Marina Mall amongst others. we had a plaza view room which easily fitted a third rollaway bed into it. we ate at the brunch restaurant which serves pizza, grilled food and late breakfast like pancakes etc. excellent service and portions. the other restaurants all looked a bit formal for a child at the hotel. the hotel was beautifully decorated for christmas. its location, opening onto the shopping mall is fab. great nibbles at gloria jeans coffee shop for brekkie. the pool and surroundings are also very good, free fruit, newspapers and use of suncream etc. my only watch out would be that they are doing some renovations at the moment and we stayed on the 28th floor and they were doing them above. they don't start till 10am and stop by about 4pm but with jet lag we were woken up a couple of times by drilling etc. i am sure that it won't last long though and the standards at the hotel more than made up for the inconvience of early noise. i would highly recommend this hotel.

<Author>menome
<Content>Great overall hotel Stayed at the Pan Pacific for 2 nights at the end of December. Got in at 6am, was really tired, however the reception noticed this and we were allowed to check in straight away. (probably because there was a room available already, but it was a very good gesture and gave a good first impression). Everything at this hotel seemed very organised, all staff knew what they were supposed to do, thus made it a very smooth trip in terms of hotel stuff ie. newspapers, wake up call, laundary, concierge.The rooms were very impressive, I believe they have just been through a renovation and everything was brand new. The rooms had a very classy/classic look and feel (some hotels can go overboard with the modern look) but I still prefer classic. Pan Pacific was like a modern classic look, if that makes sense. (had 32 inch LCD TV and electronic blinds [modern], wood finish for everything else)Bathrooms were great, with seperate bathtub and shower. Shower was large, but bathtub was the usually pint size.Location was a marina bay, right next to a few shopping plazas. Was 5 mins walk from the bay, was a nice walk and had some restaurant and hawker centres there too.Overall, this was a great and accommodating hotel, I rate it as the best place I have stayed at so far (probably in line with Mandarin Oriental, I have previously stayed at Mandarin Oriental and Swissotel Stamford)

<Author>davo2005
<Content>Absolutely wonderful Just returned from a week's stay at the Pan Pacific and strongly recommend this great hotel. If you crave superior customer service as well as first class facilities this is the hotel for you.From the moment we arrived the friendliness of the staff and the quality of their service was apparent. From the door men to the personal check-in to our room the level of service exceeded all expectations. We really appreciated the friendliness and help received from all staff during our stay.The rooms have been tastefully refurbished and have a contemporary feel. The LCD tv was a nice touch and the king bed was huge and well comfy. We felt very comfortable throughout our stay. Another nice touch was the option of clearing out the bar fridge and using it to store your own beverages etc. Very helpful.We ordered room service on a few occassions and the timing was impeccable, most efficient we have experienced. The food was good too and the fact that the in room dining menu includes items from some of the hotel's in house restaurants is fantastic.The location of the hotel couldnt be better. The hotel is linked by walkways, overpasses etc to the major shopping centres (Millenia Walk, Marina Square, Suntec City) and hotels within Marina Bay. You are basically a few minutes walk to great shopping and food. If you like to walk the Esplanade is a 10 min walk and a futher 10-15 mins will take you to Boat Quay, the museums etc. If walking isnt your thing then jump in a taxi from the hotel foyer. We never waited for a taxi no matter what time of the day and normally spent between $5-10 a fare, the furthest we travelled was to Orchard Rd. Cheap in our eyes.We had an absolutely fantastic time in Singapore and the fact that the hotel is in such a great location and the facilities and staff exceeded our expectations it just made our trip that bit more memorable.

<Author>Psycho-Badger
<Content>Quality hotel with a major caveat This was my second stay at the pan pacific, and the experience was identical on both occasions: lovely room and faultless service, but the standard of the food was very disappointing. We never had breakfast due to early check-outs both times. The first time (September 2006) we ate dinner in the French-style bistro upstairs- the food was cold, uninspiring and overpriced. On our second visit we arrived late so we ate from an asian tapas-style menu in the lobby bar- once again the food was luke warm (I doubt it was prepared fresh) and overpriced. Our bill came to 150 Singapore dollars for 4 glasses of beer and approximately six small tapas servings. I would be unlikely to pay these prices in Dublin, where I live, and Dublin is generallly regarded as one of the most expensive cities in the world.In summary then, the rooms and desk staff at the PP Singapore are excellent, and I have received good deals on the internet on both occasions. I would strongly advice against eating there however. Considering that the restaurant experience is important to me and that there is a competitive hotel market in Singapore, I don't feel the PP as a whole is up to scratch and therefore would not recommend it.

<Author>Carpinteria
<Content>Adequate but stinky I was put in this hotel by Singapore Airlines after I missed a connection due to their late flight. They assured me it is the hotel they use for first class passengers (though I was only in business class on the flight). I arrived in the early evening and left the next morning, so my experience was limited. However, three things particularly struck me about the hotel:1. There was no way to get the guest room to a high enough temperature to be comfortable,2. Though I was told that the entire hotel was non-smoking, the room in which I was placed had clearly been a smoking room very recently, because I not only couldn't rest well, but I became physicall ill and could barely breathe because of the smell of stale cigarette smoke, and3. The buffet breakfast is one of the best breakfasts I've ever had at a hotel. Indeed, my room service dinner the night before was bountiful, beautiful, and reasonably priced, so the terrific breakfast was simply the next food installment. I won't stay here again (there's a Conrad a short distance away), and had I known how pervasive and persistent the cigarette smell would be, I would have moved (but I was already tired and foolishly thought that it would go away or I would become used to it). I can see that this has the potential for a very good hotel; I simply don't think my experience there was a pleasant one, and my assessment of the property, therefore, is probably much more negative than the hotel generally merits.

<Author>StaffordKod
<Content>Great hotel My wife and I stayed at the Pan Pacific for two nights in June 2007 as part of our honeymoon. The atrium of the hotel is something to behold, it is the biggest atrium in Asia.The welcome we received at the hotel was superb, really personal service. I would definately recommend this place to honeymooners, they made us feel very special.If you want some decent panoramic photos of the Singapore sky line then take a ride in the glass elevators on the outdside of the hotel. They take you to the very top of the hotel giving you amazing views, especially at night.It is in a good location, Raffles is a 10 minutes walk away, there is a shopping centre attached to the hotel and Orchard Street and Clarkes Quay are a five minute taxi ride away. Taxi's are cheap and a good way to see the city when it is really humid. The locals are really friendly and do not try to rip you off.China town is good, probably the most civilised I have ever been to!Clarkes Quay is worth a visit too, great nightlife, loads of venues to choose from.Our only regret is that we did not stay longer. Would definately go back and stay at the Pan Pacific.

<Author>MollyCardiff
<Content>Good hotel, but a bit disappointed We stayed at the Pan Pacific en route back to the UK from Australia, having previously stayed at Raffles the Plaza on the first leg of the journey (please see my other review).Maybe my expectations were too high following our stay at Raffles the Plaza.We had paid extra for a deluxe king bed balcony room, check-in at 10.30pm on Tuesday was busy but efficient. We were given the key for a room on the 13th floor. Waited about 10 mins to get in a lift, and then found the room had twin beds. I called reception, and this was sorted out quickly and efficiently without any question and we were moved to a new room on the 15th floor.The room was nice, but a bit bland. Bathroom has a small bath, small separate shower and a partioned toilet, so good for sharing. The balcony is large, no balcony furniture (seems to be typical in Singapore), but concrete, so even if you drag chairs outside you can't sit and admire the view. The view overlooking the bay and the Oriental hotel was great. The bed was huge, but not very comfortable and the bed-linen was quite worn. Good Flat screen TV and a small mini-bar area, not very well stocked.Music from the ground-floor bar was quite loud, but did stop well before midnight. The really annoying thing was the pinging noise from the lifts that could be clearly heard from the room, even though we were the other side of the atrium from the lift shafts! Luckily we are both heavy sleepers... Maybe the rooms and the noise levels in the suites on the top floors of the hotel are better.The main lobby area of the hotel is huge, impressive to look at but a bit cold and impersonal. As expected, the hotel was full of business travellers, they hold a lot of conferences here. As tourists, we stuck out like sore thumbs in (smart) casual clothes, and didn't feel we fitted in as well as at Raffles the Plaza.The pool area and the bar next to it was gorgeous - complementary towels and water was a nice touch. Very clean, serene area with a huge beautiful pool. The spa next to it was ok, although my husband was in agony after his sports massage!I tried the room service one evening, and was very impressed - fantastic meal, excellent service and presentation, reasonable prices.The hotel is one of four hotels connected to the Marina Square mall which is huge (great food court upstairs) and next to Suntec City which is even bigger, so good for shopping, and is walking distance to the bay areas, Boat Quay, the business district etc. We popped into the other hotels to have a look, they all have the same large lobby / atrium design with similar 'bullet' lifts. The whole area just seemed a bit to similar, miles of the same thing.Overall, I loved Singapore (please see my other review for tourist tips) and this was a good hotel, but for the price I expected better, and there are more interesting areas of the city to stay in.  
<Date>Oct 27, 2007

<Author>FirstClass59
<Content>Pacific Club Rooms First stay at the Pan Pacific. I was travelling alone on Business. Since there are a number of reviews on the hotel I thought I would focus on the Pan Pacific Club Floor. Simply, the Hotel and Staff were excellent. The Club floor rooms are on upper floor of the Hotel providing outstanding views of the city. Upon arriving at the hotel you go the the Pacific Club Desk and are then escorted to a private checkin area on the 33rd floor. The elevators to the checkin desk are on the exterior face of the building offering spectacular views of the city. Upon checkin you will be greeted by the most hospitable of hosts who will remember you name the entire stay. You will recieve a cool fresh fruit drink and towel while being quickly checked in. Staying on the Pacific Club floor offers a number of ammenities that make it worth the additional price. First there are lounges on the 33rd and 34th floor for Pan Pacific Club guests. The 33rd Floor Lounge is open 24 hours with complimentary coffee, tea , juice and light snacks. Complimentary is the theme while staying on these floors... Choice of breakfast is served on the 33rd floor ( American) , the Lobby Lounge ( Continental) ; Global Kitchen Restaurant ( Buffet) or in-room dining. There is afternoon tea ( 3-5PM), Cocktails and Hors d'Oeuvres ( 5:30-7 PM) and Liquor Service ( 8-10) on the 34th Floor Club. In addition there is a complimentary in-room mini-bar stocked daily with beer, Liquor, water and soda. Internet access and local calls as well as the pressing of 3 garments are also complementary. The rooms are very spacious and well appointed. Plenty of storage as there are two closets and numerous dresser draws. There is an ironing board and iron in each room. The room has a large flat panel TV and DVD player. The Bathroom is very large and luxurious. Marble everywhere. L'occitane bath products , hair dryer, shaving kits , tooth brush and paste are included. There is a seperate shower and bath. There are a number of very good restaurants in the hotel. Even with all the ammenties the outstanding service throughout the hotel is what really stood out.

<Author>Skeoughs
<Content>Outstanding We always check reviews on this site but have never written one, except it would be wrong not to say how amazing this hotel is. To be honest it was part of a 2 day stay over in Singapore on the way back from Oz so we didnt really care where Trailfinders put us, but from the moment we walked into the lobby and saw the Blade Runner type lifts we were enthralled. The room was extremely comfortable, we cannot have feathers in the duvet etc, which they had, but on ringing the concierge the whole bed linen was changed within 20mins.We have to mention 2 of the fantastic restaurants in this hotel.One was serving thier local food for breakfast, hot with all the sauces, I've never eaten so much (an Im usually a cereal person) but the Indian restaurant was outstanding, we have never eaten so well. Unfortunately when we were staying it was the last few days before it was being re-decorated and they were closing off the kitchens from viewing which we think will be a pity.The pool (as you can see from the pics) was an excellent size and the gym was extremely well equipped.On our last day we did some sight seeing and obviously had checked out, but we were provided with towels for showering and freshening up in their beautiful changing rooms beside the pool.This is defenitely the best hotel we have stayed in for quite some time and we would absolutely recommend it to anyone who wants and excellent hotel is a superb location within walking distance of the major malls and Raffles.

<Author>rmwhitt
<Content>Good location, especially for shoppers The Pan Pacific is located in Marina Square, adjacent to a shopping mall that connects to another shopping mall that connects to another shopping mall, and another...well, you get the picture. Singapore is known for its shopping opportunities and this hotel allows both the shopper and the sightseer to enjoy themselves. You can literally walk for miles underground, or surface and visit the Esplanade (river area) or Boat Quay/Clark Quay before returning to airconditioned spendor of the vast underground.I travel to Singapore every year and this is my first stay at Pan Pacific. If you like to walk, you can get around the city on foot easily from this hotel, or you can use the MRT/public transport (train) which is very user friendly. Taxis are very inexpensive but traffic can be tough. The hotel was very nice, a good 4*. I snagged it at a great rate of US$120 when other hotels (lesser or equal ones) cost $180 or more. It's comparable to Swissotel and better than the M or the Amara. The room was a good size, soothing in decor. It was typically outfitted in standard 4* comforts. Big shower stall was a pleasure to use (no tub). The outdoor pool was nice, as was the dry sauna in the pool area.I did not eat in the hotel but there are a couple of restaurants and an active lobby bar with singer/entertainment at night.Service was attentive and pleasant.

<Author>terravisum
<Content>Very nice hotel My flight comes in a bit early around 8AM and the quick cab ride to the Pan Pacific got me into the hotel lobby around 9AM.As it was early, I was notified by the front desk that my room was not ready and promptly invited me to the lobby lounge/bar for a complimentary drink while the hotel setting up my room. One cup of cappuccino later and I was invited to check out my room.The room was a good size room with a large King bed. I have a nice view to the Marina and can see the Merlion from my window. The bed was comfortable and clean. Probably one of the best hotel room that I have seen so far aside from the Singapore Grand Hyatt.The walk-in bathroom is a large size with separate shower and bathtub. The room is stocked with standard amenities of shampoo, conditioner and lotion. A complimentary shoeshine service is also available as part of the room. There are live band music every night from 7PM-11PM in the lobby and since the Pan Pacific is an atrium-type hotel, if you like to sleep early and have issues with sounds, you might want a high-floor room. There are bird-chirping sound in the atrium in the morning but I think they are just sounds playing from loudspeaker than real live birds.Turned-down service is done everyday around 6PM. The service is attentive with an accent on security. There are always several security guards manning the entrance from outside to the connecting entrance from the shopping complex nearby.The location is a bit off from Orchard road but it has good way to get on the freeway to the airport.

<Author>OldBear
<Content>A Great Hotel, Dont Miss Out! What a great Hotel. We stayed here at the end of March 07 for three nights. Having travelled from the UK with Singapore Airlines we used our 'Boarding Pass Privelage' to book an offer direct with the hotel which included breakfast. We arrived direct from the airport at 08:00 hours and asked if there was 'any likelyhood' of checking in early as check in time is 3 pm. We were given our room at 10.45am.Breakfast at the hotel is buffet style with an extensive range of foods to suit all. We were on the 19th floor and had an excellent view of the river and city district. Yes we could hear the music and singing, but it ends before midnight, so why not go down to the bar and enjoy? Alcohol in Singapore IS expensive especially wine, but then you do not see any drunkeness on the streets.The location of the 'Pan Pac' is excellent for the Marina Shopping Centre and the MRT. The MRT is an underground train system which is Very safe and cheap.The hotel rooms are spacious, clean and have very comfortable large beds. There is a business centre on a higher floor which allows you use of a computer and Internet for a small charge.There is a 'tour desk' on the 2nd floor where you can book many different trips including the Night Safari. Don't miss Swimming with the Dolphins at Sentosa Island ( Book at .'Underwaterworld' before you go for only 拢50 each.)

<Author>Lizzy-Lee
<Content>Very nice hotel I stayed here for 4 nights over Easter and had a pleasant stay. Got a fantastic deal through a travel agent making it very good value for money so shop around as even expedia couldn't better it.Generally I find that with hotels it is not the problems but the solutions that can make all the difference and the Pan Pacific dealt well with the issues that came up.The first room I was given had a locked connnecting door to another room through which a lot of noise from the children there could be heard. One call to reception and they quickly moved me to another room without fuss.However the air con in the 2nd room was noisy and cold - again this was repaired quickly when I reported it. The Concierge and reception were all friendly and helpful. The breakfast in the Global Kitchen restaurant was extensive and vey good quality - local expat friends joining me felt it was good value for SNG $35I can see noise from the atium might be an issue on lower floors but only when there is a singer or musician in the lobby bar which is not late or every night. Nice rooms, spacious bathrooms and good toiletries including hair conditioner which was a plus. There is a big pool and gym area which is really nice and well serviced. It felt very safe having to use your room card to access bedroom floors. The atrium is pretty spectacular and gives the hotel a bit of a edge. The bakery/deli even had Hot cross Buns on sale.Having direct access to a huge shopping mall is a plus if you love shopping. There is a Carrefour supermarket in Suntec mall to buy fresh milk, juice or anything else you like and a good food hall next door in the other mall for a cheap lunch. Would certainly stay again if I could get a similar price.

My flight was not leaving until early evening and I was encouraged to wait in the hotel for as long as I wished and to avail myself of all the facilities of the pacific floor, including afternoon tea.When I took a taxi to the airport I was overcharged by the taxi driver but even this negative has been changed into a positive by the wonderful staff of Pan Pacific. The hotel is in a good location connected to an enormous modern air conditioned shopping mall through which you can walk right into town and the nearest MRT ( underground train) station. The hotel is also very helpful in letting you check in early morning after a long flight from Europe.One small complaint. Due to the hollow atrium of the hotel (which is very spectacular), the noise from a resident singer and band at the cocktail lounge on the ground floor can be heard in the rooms on the lower floors in the evenings. The singing seems to, however, stop at midnight and it is not that loud.

<Author>HinduMystic
<Content>The Pan Pacific - Cool, Quite and Convenient and definately worth Consideration Due to the lack of double beds at the Mandarin Oriental, we decided to stay at he Pan Pacific and it was an excellent choice.We were in Singapore to celebrate my wife's 40th birthday and our 1st Wedding Anniversary.Check-in was quick and efficient and the Hotel kindly upgraded our room as it was my wife's birthday. They sent a delicious Cake and flowers to our room on the day of her birthday which was a nice touch.The Rooms are nice and airy with a huge comfortable bed. Floor to celing window means you can see Singapore out side and the views are great.All the rooms have wireless Internet access and you can use the Business floor if you need to but this can be a bit expensive.The hotel staff are excellent and polite. We didn't have to call anyone for anything the whole time we were there. Sit out in shaded comfort and have some food at Brunch on the 4th Floor, The pool is just around the corner, They do all-day breakfast for those that missed breakfast, which we did everyday!!!The Indian restaraunt Rang Mahal was closed for refurbishement, but all the food places were execellent as wellThe Atruim Bar can get very busy after 5.00pm but its a cool place to have a drinks and chill out and listen to the live musicThe hotel is in a really good location, right next to two malls, Marina Plaza and Suntec City Mall, the later being the bigger and having a superb selection of restaurants.We would definately stay here again and would have no hesitation in recommending this to any readers out thereThe City Hall MRT station is a short walk away and if you cut through the City Link Mall, you can get to it in air-conditioned comfort.Buy an EZ-Link Pass if you plan to use the MRT as it will save you money and if you hand it in after you finish with it you get 3SD back plus any money still left on the card.Things to do while in Singapore:Sentosa Island - Go by Cable car and wonder around the island. Go during the week to avoid the crowdsChinatown/Little India - experience some of the culture and shoppingBukit Timah Nature Reserve Trek through the only tropical Rainforest in Singapore.Take lots of water and prepare to climb lots of stepsNight Safari Fun and well organised night out to see some of the animals that you dont normally get to see. Take a cab to the Zoo...it's a lot easier and costs about 11-15 SGD. Try and get something to eat early as the restaurants at the Night Safari close abour 11-1130pmOrchard RoadShopping, shopping and more shoppingSIM LIM Square For All your electronics stuff ...remember to haggle!Raffles Singapore Sling at the Long Bar- overated, but has to be doneDrinks at the Axis Lounge, Mandarin Oriental HotelEnjoy a drink in the chic, intimate atmosphere where you can listen to cool downtempo tunes while watching Singapore at night.

<Author>pusspuss
<Content>Very comfortable hotel in convenient location I would happily return to teh Pan Pacific any time. In fact, we tried to work out whether we'll afford to live there instead of paying two mortgages back home. It was sooo comfortable. Arrived late am from an overnight train journey looking a bit ruffled. We were offered a room there and then, although not our choice, and decided to wait for a double and asked for a place to change. Amazingly, we were then whisked to a day room where we could shower and change, and upon or return alter, out luggage had been taken to our room. On the fire-escape plan I could see it was the smallest room on the floor, but is was also a corner room with a good view and zero noise, and still spacious. I agree with one of the previous posters that the decor is a bit dated, but the rooms have been nicely updated with more contemporary fabric, ultra-comfy Aeron work chairs and stylish desk lamps. Yes, the atrium with its fake plants screams 1980's yuppie abode, I am not sure about the quaint artwork in the communal areas and above our bed, and I would have loved to rip out the crumpled old rubber shower curtain that was like an ugly pimple in our otherwise sumptuous marble bathroom. We also ate at the Chinese restaurant and visited the pool many times. The Chinese restaurant is on the 37th floor and while the decor is really bland and the floor doesn't revolved and the windows are misted up so you cannot see out very well the food here is phantastic. Singapore is generally a good place to eat, and food is plentiful and cheap in many food centres, but this was many notches up and justified the comparably high price. The pool area was nice, shape of the pool a little naff, not good for laps, but clean water and not too chlorinated. There were harldy ever any other people in the pool so I feel its size is adequate even for a large hotel like this. I kept looking out for the Marina MRT station which is already printed in my 2003 LP guide, but unfortunately its still a 15 min walk through airconditioned malls to the nearest MRT at City Hall. Also, if travelling on leisure, it may be better to have a lie-in, as many shops and the excellent Marina Food loft open only at 10am.

<Author>G2WestLothian
<Content>Honeymoon Part 1 We stayed in this hotel in Singapore for the first part of our honeymoon, for four nights. The hotel looked after us very well with flowers and a beautiful chocolate cake on arrival, as well as an upgrade to a balcony room. The room was spacious, with a large bed and exceptionally clean. There were bathrobes and slippers in the room and towels were changed twice a day. The hotel atrium is spectacular and the hotel is well situated for sightseeing, eating out and shopping. There were a number of restaurants in the hotel. We went to the Chinese one on the 37th floor on the first night and perhaps the only thing we didn't like was the way they served the food as compared with what our palate is used to. We were not long off the flight and not too hungry, so ordered soup to start and then 1/2 Crispy Peking Duck for main to share. Only the duck skin was served in the pancakes and after we finished that we got our duck meat mixed with noodles (although we felt this had been taken from a sparrow, as there was not much meat at all!). One afternoon we had food by the pool which was delicious and another evening we had room service and although we only had burgers and wedges - they were fantastic. The hotel also has pool and spa facilities. We used the pool, which has amazing underwater acoustics, but didn't use the spa facilities. Anytime we called the concierge, we found them very helpful.The hotel is also aimed at the business traveller and I found that it catered well for those on business and on leisure. All the staff were very friendly and efficient. I would definitely come to this hotel again if in Singapore and have recommended it to a friend already - who is going in February!

<Author>G&RCheshire
<Content>A great hotel for a honeymoon ever! We stayed here over the Christmas period as the first half of our honeymoon.Our first impressions of the hotel were excellent. We were met from the taxi by a doorman in pristine, traditional dress who whisked our suitcases away and delivered them to our room promptly. Check-in could not have been better and the bunch of red roses we were given were stunning.The room was immaculate and, in my opinion, not at all dated. The bed was immense and extremely comfortable and all of the fixtures and fittings were up-to-date as well as classy. Everyone we came across in the hotel (reception, room service, concierge, cleaning and bar staff) were extremely polite, professional and friendly.The hotel is in a great position in Singapore. It is linked to two good malls and there are plenty of places to eat in both of them. It is within easy walking distance of the Esplanade Theatre on the Bay which is a lovely area down by the water. The only very minor bad point is the MTR building work going on around the hotel at the moment. So you have to learn quickly how to navigate your way through the malls to walk anywhere!Overall, it is a top-quality hotel where we were made to feel like royalty whilst on our honeymoon!
