<Author>Acker
<Content>Great End to a Memorable Trip This was the final hotel on our round-the-world trip, and did not disappoint. A friend recommended it, and was proved right to do so. We arrived for a 3-night stay late in the evening, and were checked-in and whisked off to our room in a trice. I had, I confess, alerted the hotel to the fact that this was a trip to celebrate our Silver Wedding anniversary, and, unbeknownst to my wife, had asked by e-mail for some flowers in our room, for which I would happily pay. The hotel staff were great, and she got her flowers at the front desk, plus a card. Once installed in a room with a balcony, and a great view of the Merlion in the inner harbour, - this was a free upgrade - we were then surprised by room service who delivered fruit, a cake, and a bottle of champagne!! This set the tone, and we continued to be impressed with the friendliness and helpful attitude of all staff. We breakfasted twice in the Global Kitchen restaurant, which, although not too cheap, and not included in the room price, was excellent. Its worth noting that the price for this is the same whether you eat a large or small breakfast. The pool was very clean, but beware having too many drinks or refreshments there if your budget is a bit slim. Once we checked out -  we asked for a late one as our flight was at 1130pm, the concierge's boys put our bags into secure storage, and we spent some time at the pool bar enjoying a beer. If you opt to have the poolside BBQ dinner, the beer is on free-flow, but - alas! our schedule precluded that meal. We had no complaints at all, and would happily go back any time.

<Author>jencenny
<Content>Excellent hotel in a great location We stayed at the Pan Pacific for 4 nights and thought it was overall, an excellent hotel. Check in was quick and we got given a room on the eighteenth floor which had a balcony with magnificent harbour views. The buffet breakfast was good with a wide selection of international cuisines to choose from. The Atrium bar was on the pricey side but the service was excellent. The best thing about the hotel is it's location. Its about a ten minute walk through air conditioned shopping arcades to the nearest MRT station and even less of a walk to the Esplanade.  I would highly recommend it and would definately stay there again.

<Author>divinzia
<Content>Fantastic service, slightly retro (70s) feel, but comfortable. Good gym. Stayed here for a major international meeting in late September. The room rate was somewhat inflated (S$450) but then the entire city held the participants hostage to higher rates. Check-in efficient and friendly. Lobby was slightly retro and jarring in style and a touch dark. Very expensive drinks at the bar and very limited food service anywhere outside the formal restaurants. The rooms were nicely modern and thoughtfully appointed with, at least in my case, a great view. If you are a towering-inferno fear of heights person, however, you won't want to get into the glass pod that zooms up and down to the 25+ floors ... you have been warned.Bathrooms were fine but nothing exceptional. The rest of the room, however, made up for it.Very well equipped gym (although some magazines and less loud-talking radio [more music] would be helpful). Nice pool.Highlight of the culinary aspect was the fantastic indian restaurant here which was one of the best indian meals I have ever had (this from a UK lass who prides herself in hunting down the best curries!). Other (discriminating) friends went to the rooftop Cantonese restaurant and were also impressed.Overall, definitely above average, particularly for the business traveler. Not sure if it would be my destination for a holiday, but perhaps, with some sensible prices.

<Author>MD6_UK
<Content>Well positioned, helpful staff. No nonsense business hotel based about 20 mins (and 20 dollars) away from airport. Hotel and area recommended by ex pat friend. Couldnt fault price or service. Rooms are immaculate and fairly spacious with plenty of little touches that help weary travellers (toothbrushes, washing powder sachet etc).Hotel is attached to Marina Square mall. From there you can get to the Suntec centre easily without venturing out into the tropical heat. Marina Square has wide range of shops and boutiques including useful large supermarket.Staff attentive when needed - we had them looking after various combinations of bags whilst we travelled. They also do 3pm checkouts for free where availability allows. The use of a room for three hours costs about 30 sing dollars if you need to freshen up on travel days.Internet access is expensive at around 8 sing dollars for 15 mins plus print costs on top.Stylish bar is expensive but is on par with similar hotels around the Island (beer about 14 dollars per bottle, cocktails about 16). It looks good but is one for those on expenses only. Cannot comment on hotel restaurants. Restaurants in Marina square are very good and very cheap. They are certainly not top end and there are a lot of chains (genki sushi etc) however the food is exemplary. For a really cheap meal venture to the food court especially the stall that specialises in the chinese meats.This hotels would suit business travellers and tourists who want a little bit more from a hotel and those who want to be away from the hub bub of Orchard Road. Would not suit those who expect ultra luxury ie the type who like to be carried to their rooms.

<Author>beijau
<Content>Good location, good value Although I normally stay at the Fullerton and prefer to stay at the Four Seasons, when the money is coming out of my own pocket I have a soft spot for the Pan Pac.The rooms are fine, the beds are fine, and room service delivers promptly. I do agree that the reception staff are not to be commended for their customer service efficiency. Oh well, smile and think of the price you're paying.The same atrium design that I find so cheesy in their San Francisco property kind of works in Singapore. I haven't taken issue with the lighting, by the way; the overall design is not much of an issue unless you want to spend your time inside. With so much air conditioned real estate including untold hectares of shopping malls to be found elsewhere in the Lion City, why hang out here except maybe for champagne in the lounge?Well, let me answer my own question. The spa is competitive on features (lots of rooms, massage treatments), price, and availability. Try getting a massage booking on the weekend in Singapore without many days' advance notice. Good luck! But I like this spa so much I buy discounted block tickets and go back while staying at those other hotels.The Marina Square location is great for working at Suntec City, and a short cab to the business district. No complaints there.If you get a good deal on the room, stay here. If you have to pay up or you are on an expense account, you can do better.

<Author>Reissunainen
<Content>Who turned out the lights? The Pan Pacific is marketed as a high range business hotel with luxurious accommodation and top facilities. While the room was beautiful, as was the view, I could not get over the darkness in the lobby and other public areas. The design of the hotel is quite unique, but having the lights dimmed throughout just gives it a gloomy overall impression - as if the power went off and the back-up generator kicked in! I was also unimpressed by the efficiency of the reception staff as it took forever to check in and out. Also, I had specifically booked an exceptionally early check-in, but as I showed up the hotel was experiencing delays and unexpectadly full and I had to wait for 2 hours in the lobby for a room to be vacated. While this is understandable, I would have expected a hotel of this standard to have a Plan B for waiting visitors, ie. a lounge or something. And finally, the Summerhouse restaurant was being renovated during my stay, which meant non-stop drilling and banging noise from 10am to 10pm. So, even though many things at this hotel are excuisite, the experience was not all that great.

<Author>Mancunian Steve
<Content>Great Experience I have just returned from Singapore for a 3 night stay and had a great time in the Pan Pacific Hotel.I arrived off a long flight from Europe at 8am in the morning and was expecting to be told that I couldnt check into my room until the afternoon which is normal practice, was really surprised as quite the reverse happened and I was upgraded to a suite for my stay as there were no normal rooms available!!!.The hotel was slightly more expensive than I normally pay for my stays in singapore but I had the special package which included $40 a day credit with the hotels bars which made it a competiive deal, and the hotel is well worth it with an amazing atrium, great pool / Gym and an excellant choice of restuarants.My only gripe was that the free breakfast offered as part of the package was continental style, which was very good but did not include cooked items like bacon, eggs and sausages for which you had to pay about $5 extra.The Hotel is connected to the Marina Mall and is about ten mins walk to the Raffles hotel and Chijmes bar / Restaurant complex ( great place for a night out ! )The main thing I will remember though are the staff, they are everywhere you go, incredibly helpful and really make your stay here five starred. Overall an excellant experience and as long as I can get the package deal again I will definitely be returning.

<Author>Fondofgoodtravel
<Content>Very Pleasant Stay We wanted a relaxing and peaceful 4 night stopover en route to New Zealand. Relaxing and peaceful not being the words I'd choose to describe Singapore but we were well aware of this! For this reason we opted to avoid hotels in the Orchard Road area and Marina Bay seemed a quieter area.We arrived at about 8am in the morning absolutely exhausted and we hoped and prayed that the PP would be able to find us a room although we were aware that if they ahd every right to turn us away till the check in time of 3pm. Reception staff were extremely accommodating and said a room would be ready in an hour. Check in was slow but the fact that we wre promised a room in an hour and were given free late check out meant that everything was forgiven!We sat in the bar area and ordered 2 soft drinks - definitely not cheap! Looking up at the lifts was entertaining for an hour and before long our room was ready. The room was quite typical large, corporate hotel style. King size bed, fridge, water, tea and coffee, safe, room to put the cases, bath robes, slippers and a decent view of the skyscrapers. Bathroom was large - deep tub as well as shower cubicle. The bed was extremely comfortable or that could have been due to the 18 hr flight we'd had!Pool area was pleasant enough - not the largest but loungers were clean and it provided respite in the midst of the bustling city. We ate one night at Hai Tien Lo, the Chinese restaurant on the 37th floor and had to take the exterior lifts all the way up. First time up I had to close my eyes and could feel my knees trembling but after that had several trips just to enjoy the views! Food was absolutely delicious - expensive meal but worth it. Try the cod in Moet and Chandon sauce - perfect! Service was subtle and non intrusive. The whole meal was a lovely experience and very romantic.There was building work going on around the hotel which did make walking difficult but walking in Singapore is always difficult given the stifling heat. That's the why the cheap taxis are so great!Go for Sunday champagne brunch at the Ritz Carlton ($50 per head) which is truly an experience. Unlimited vintage Moet champagne, lobster, sushi, 10 different types of oysters, roast meats, ommelettes to order, hot food, 63 different cheeses, white and dark chocolate souffles to order, numerous desserts... Expensive but such value for money!

<Author>char645
<Content>Fantastic hotel with minor problems This was my first trip to Asia and the third continent I've ever set foot on (unless if you consider Europe and Asia one continent.) I walked into the atrium, and it's the absolute most gorgeous and colorful hotel atrium I've seen! The staff was plesant and cooperative. They gave us free breakfast at the Summer House every morning, one of seven restaurants in hotel itself. The elevators are also a marvel, especially the outside ones, although they face the hotel side of the town, not downtown. When I finally got into the room, I liked the nice oversized doors and key holder, but I was slightly dissapointed at how small the room seemed. The room itself (excluding the bathroom) was also quite blank and lacking color unlike the rest of the hotel. The deluxe rooms did look a little better by judging at its photos on their website. The executive centre was a nice way to keep in touch and e-mail people at home. The other nice feature was the connecting corridor to Suntec City Mall and the fourth floor garden. As for the restaurants, they were decent. The coffee wasn't that good at the Summer House, but the tea and fruit were fabulous! We also had cocktails at the Atrium Lounge, which came with an odd assortment of snacks: dried calamari, mustard coated peas, and (sigh) mixed nuts. It may or may not be the custom, but nevertheless, it seemed strange to us. Overall, it was a satisfying hotel with minor problems.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Absolutely fantastic hotel Having stayed in many other Singapore hotels, I thought I'd give Pan Pacific a try as I like the Marina Bay area and also that expedia were offering very attractive rates.What an amazing hotel! From the moment you check in, you are treated with such fantastic customer service and made to feel really at home.The lobby is spectacular with fancy lighting, angles and sparkling glass lifts going up and down. My room was on the 32nd floor with the best view of downtown Singapore I have ever seen. My room itself was also beautiful - really spacious with massive bed, TV and really stunning bathroom.I was on the leisure package which includes SGD$40 per day worth of food and beverages and so I had quite a bit of room service. The food was absolutely delicious and reasonably priced.I went to the gym a couple of times and was pleasantly surprised at the good selection and excellent condition of the equipment. The pool was also great.Had a few cocktails in the Atrium bar which were very good, but a little pricey at nearly $20 per drink.The location of the hotel is great - it's right by 3 big shopping malls so you have immediate access to all the shops you want (bring a big suitcase with you). There is also very easy access to the Central Business District (5 minutes in a taxi) and it's close to the river with the Boat Quay and Clarke Quay restaurants. If you want to be near Orchard Road, chose a different hotel, but I really prefer the Marina Bay location as there is more variety of things to do. And in any case, even if you do want to go to Orchard Road it's only about 10-15 mins in a taxi.All in all, this hotel is one of the best I have ever stayed in. Real luxury and fantastic service at affordable prices.

<Author>CSET
<Content>An excellent start to a holiday of a lifetime Stayed at the Pan Pacific for 2 nights in March 2006 and we were impressed from the moment we arrived - although I would agree that the reception staff weren't overly cheery and personal.Upgraded our room (as appears to be the norm) to one on the 17th floor with a seaview and the most amazing view of Singapore. The bed was huge as was the bath, and the room a good size and clean. Loved the fact that the hotel was attached to the Marina Square Mall, and the walk to City Mall MRT took no time at all. The bar / reception area of the hotel is lovely, the glass lifts making it very attractive. We didn't eat at the hotel but we did have drinks in the bar - they were expensive, but we expected that, and the bar had a nice atmosphere and the waitresses looked stunning and they and the bar staff were very friendly.We used the pool on 3 occasions and went to the gym once. Take a bottle of water with you and don't expect it to be huge, but there were enough machines for a decent work out. The pool area is attractive with nice sunloungers and a very clean pool. In all we loved it at this hotel. It was a stopover on our way to New Zealand and we were were glad we chose to stay here.

<Author>Riverfrog
<Content>Very nice central hotel in downtown Singapore We stayed for 8 days/7 nights at the Pan Pacific Hotel in downtown Singapore in March 2006. It was our first trip to Singapore, so we did not know what to expect. Thankfully, we enjoyed our stay very much. We checked in to our hotel on the 20th floor, a non-smoking room with a king sized bed. It was nice, spacious, and very clean.The best thing about the hotel is its easy access to public transportation. To get from the hotel to the City Hall MRT (train) station, you don't even need to walk outside, just through air-conditioned malls and walkways. The MRT takes you almost everywhere you could want to go, although for some of the more far-out places (like the Zoo or Bird Park), a cab is quite cheap and is easy to get from the front of the hotel. We took a cab from the hotel to the airport in the early morning and it only cost S$14.The Pan Pacific is located in the Marina Square Mall. If you love shopping, there are two other malls all within walking distance and connected to each other (Suntec City Mall and Raffles City Mall). Make sure to visit the Fountain of Wealth in the Suntec City Mall and follow the ritual! Also, take advantage of the many money changers in the mall. Try to get small bills if you can ($5 and smaller) to use for train fare as change is limited to $4.The hotel is very centrally located to everything. It is walking distance to museums, malls, the Esplanade performing arts center, famous Merlion, Clarke Quay (pronouced kee for all us clueless Americans ;), riverboats, restaurants, and more. So very convenient.The hotel is beautiful, with glass elevators on both the inside and outside. Take the outside elevators all the way up to the 37th floor - the restaurant floor - for an exquisite view of the city. On the fourth floor of the hotel is a pool (which looked very nice but we did not use) with an outdoor bar and a gym (also very nice but they apparently do not have water so bring your own).Our only complaint was the loud music from the hotel bar, which was only made worse by the hotel's beautiful atrium design. The music kept going even past midnight, which surprised us because the other reviews here seemed to indicate that the bar music stopped earlier. If you are a light sleeper, or a business traveler who has to go to bed early to wake up early, you might not want to stay here. We are incredulous that management would allow music that loud to be played that late. It did not bother me as I am a pretty fast sleeper, but I woke up one day to find that my boyfriend had stuffed a towel under the door to try to minimize the sound! :(We did not find the front desk or the concierge very helpful or particularly attentive. Our room was prepaid but they tried to charge us again for some reason even though we brought the print-out receipt so be careful! As for the concierge...bring a guide book or buy one in Singapore! While maps are readily available for free at all visitors' centre, a good guide book is a must. Despite all of that, we found that our calls to their help line, ServiceOne, for wake-up calls were met with great friendliness and professionalism by Sue. Our room was impeccable, with a nice bathroom (separate shower and tub and toilet) and nice amenities. Bottles of water are provided daily, as are a free electric hotpot and instant coffee and tea packets. Very nice to start the day off with coffee and a free copy of the Straits Times! Internet access is only provided free if you upgrade to an executive floor. Otherwise, it is S$10.50 for one hour and is also offered at a lower rate for 6 hours or 24 hours. This charge seemed to me to be quite unnecessary as it was wireless anyway, and I would guess that many of their travelers are business travelers, due to its proximity to the Convention Center. Oh well.We prefer to eat outside of the hotel on trips, and so cannot rate the bar or restaurants.Finally, a word of caution. There is some construction going on somewhat near the hotel--the building of yet another train station. This construction is outside of Suntec City Mall and in my opinion is not close enough to be a noise problem. However, we felt that walking around in that area was pretty difficult, given the road closures. You can, of course, take alternate routes. We only walked around there one time, to go to visit the Raffles Hotel.All in all, the hotel is very nice. If we visit Singapore again, we would most likely try something else as there are a lot of hotel options to be had. However, the Pan Pacific is worth a first visit. We hope you have a wonderful time in Singapore!  
<Date>Apr 4, 2006

<Author>Almatt
<Content>Good base for sightseeing We stayed at the Pan Pacific for 4 nights in February. Overall, we were pleased with this hotel. On the plus side, the room was a good size as was the bathroom and they were well equipped. We were on the 12th floor and didn't hear the noise from the bar in the atrium that some have complained of. The breakfast buffet was excellent. The main bar was cool and relaxing for a drink or two (but we thought it was a bit pricey especially when tax etc was added!). The location is very good with direct air conditioned access to shopping malls and you can walk to Raffles, Boat Quay etc in about 10 mins. Taxis are very cheap in Singapore and they use meters so it was hassle-free. The PP has a nice pool area.There wasn't really too much of a down side to be quite honest but, in common with many chain hotels in large cities, the PP is a bit impersonal. That didn't bother us though as we just used it as a base. The main thing to note is the lifts! Do NOT stay here if you don't like heights. The lifts from reception to about the 22nd floor are inside the atrium of the hotel and are very impressive but they are glass sided and vertigo sufferers will freak out. If you are on a higher floor then you need to use similar lifts on the exterior of the hotel... you have been warned! Great views though if you like that sort of thing.

<Author>Simon38
<Content>Not perfect I stayed at this hotel for 2 weeks. As I was there for 2 weeks this meant I was upgraded to the residence floors, 27th floor. If you're scared of heights you won't like the lift up the outside of the building. Views from the room balcony were great though. The residence breakfast was terrible.The hotel reception atrium is very impressive. When you arrive you really think this is a great looking hotel. This is a little misleading. The rooms are a little dated, while the bathrooms are very nice, the TVs are quite old, the bed is not very comfortable and the decor is a bit faded. The wireless internet is also a bit unreliable.The hotel bar is a nice place to spend 30 minutes, no longer. There is a singer on at the bar every night and due to the atrium design they can be heard in your room even on a high floor. If you want to sleep before 11pm, good luck.The hotel restaurants are quite good, particularly the indian, but very expensive compared with the world outside the hotel.The pool is very good although the service is a bit lacking there. It's a hunt to find a towel and there are not many loungers.I've stayed in a lot of hotels in Asia and I don't think I would choose this hotel again, you can fiund perfection in Singapore and this isn't it.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Enjoyed Our Stay! My husband  I stayed at the hotel for 3 nights as part of the Singapore Stopover Holiday promotion which is really a good deal. This hotel was not really our first choice but Ritz-Carlton and Shangri-la Hotels were both booked on the days we were in Singapore. No regrets because Pan-Pacific is just superb. Although we did not get the room with the queen bed (they only have a twin-bed room at check-in), we were pleased with our room. It has nice furnitures, very clean and quite spacious. The bathroom was large, modern, classy and of course very clean. The usual 5-star amenities were there (in-room safe, slippers, bathroom robes and toiletries). We were on the 7th floor and we can faintly hear the nightly music from downstairs but it did not bother us at all. The view from our room is not the best, just buildings like the Mandarin, Marina Square, etc. I guess we can't complain since we only paid $50/person/night(I'm sure I need to pay more than that to get a top-notch view). Staff were courteous and very accommodating. Breakfast was not included in our room rate. We did not try breakfast at the hotel since they were serving American buffet. We wanted to try the local food so we were mostly eating in places around the hotel. The best part is the hotel is coveniently located and so close to shopping and commercial centers. You don't have to go too far since the hotel and shopping complexes are somehow connected to each other. We LOVED the concept since one does not have to go out (it was so hot and humid outside) and you just walk inside an airconditioned complex. Overall, we had a very lovely time at the Pan-Pacific and we will definitely stay at the Pan-Pacific Singapore whenever we find ourselves in that part of Asia.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Sets the standard for Far Eastern city hotels - "Great" Stayed at the Pan Pacific and have since recommended it agressively to anyone who will listen to me. This place has become my benchmark for all world hotels. (EG - Recently stayed at the Luxor, Las Vegas and said Not bad, but it isnt the Pan Pacific. Recently stayed at the Waldorf Astoria, New York and said  Not bad, but it is'nt the Pan Pacific.... you get the picture)ANYWAYUpon arrival, you are greeted by hotel check-in staff (not porters) and escorted across red carpet, through its lavishly decorated entrance, through to check-in. After being further escorted to your room (we had a 25th floor room with amazing cityscape views), your luggage arrives. This service continues throughout your stay (namely, after calling the concierge for a power adaptor, one arrived at my door within 3 minutes!).When we checked in, we were treated like film stars. However, the fact we had come off a 12 hour flight, stank of free booze and were dishevelled in our combat trousers, t-shirts and trainers never altered the staffs attention.As previously described, our room had awesome views down over Raffles, Orchard Road and the city sprawl beyond. The room was huge with a 7ft wide bed and an impressive marble bathroom with modern fittings.Location wise, its great. You are within minutes of the SunTec City shopping area and can walk almost half a mile from the hotel through to an adjoining shopping mall which takes you close to Raffles towards Orchard Road and the quay areas. You need to bear in mind that this half a mile walk is within the comfort of an airconditioned mall and this benefit shouldnt be dismissed in the Malaysian heat/humidity.The pool is superb, with changing area and impeccable poolside service. The inner atrium is a sight to behold and the atrium bar a classy place to have a drink before you jump in a cycle-rickshaw on your way to dinner at Boat Quay or Clarke Quay.Bear in mind, this hotel costs around 拢85 a night and undercuts nearly every hotel in the world on its value for money then surpasses so many with its service. Therefore you can see why I'm recommending this as must book for your Singapore city stopover. Please dont consider anywhere else.... you dont know what you're missing!  
<Date>Oct 21, 2005

<Author>Smeg
<Content>Pretty ordinary hotel We stayed here for 3 nights in May, 2005 as part of a Singapore Airlines Stopover Holiday. Although this is rated as 4 1/2 star, some of the rooms definitely aren't. Initially we were given a very basic room (room 905). We were told this is the standard of room given for stopovers. <Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>great deal on Singapore airways We stayed at the Pan pacific for two nights on the way back from Sydney to the UK. If you fly Singapore Airlines they do a great deal - we booked online and got a great price for a fabulous room and they included the breakfast buffet in the package as well. You have to show your boarding pass so don't lose it!! There is a lot of building work going on outside as they build a new train station - nearest one is about a 10 minute walk away through airconditioned shopping centre. This was a little confusing and also when we returned late in the evening we found ourselves locked out of the entrance we had originally used and had to make our way round the outside to the main entrance past the highway and the building works. Nevertheless we enjoyed our stay enormously - staff were couteous and efficient and even though this is a very big hotel they went out the way to treat you like individuals. Concierge was particularly helpful and personally escorted us through the hotel / shopping centre bit to show us where we needed to go. We would definately return.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Wonderful, Luxurious Hotel - Recommended! We stayed here in July 2005 for a three night stopover on the way to Australia. The hotel was recommended to me by my parents following a stay there five years earlier. Everything they said was true, even after the five year gap. The hotel offers perhaps the most luxurious rooms I have ever stayed in. The huge beds are very comfortable, the bathroom is wonderful - all frosted glass and marble, and the atrium is an eye-opener - even after a 12 hour flight.The staff are extremely polite and courteous, and while check-in did seem to take a while, they will do all they can to ensure that your stay is a comfortable one, whether travelling for business or pleasure.The buffet breakfasts were very welcome. The location was quite handy too, a 10 minute walk to the MRT, and all of this done under the air-conditioned cover of one of the many shopping malls. The drinks in the bar were very expensive and this could be seen as a downside to the hotel, but we preferred to go out for the evening anyway.I would recommend this hotel to anyone and will definitely stay there again the next time I find myself in that corner of the world.

<Author>rajukarmel
<Content>Best Hotel in Singapore We stayed at Pan Pacific Singapore in March 2005 for three nights. This was our 2nd stay at this hotel. When we arrived about 10:30am there were several people checking in. The lady that was checking us in had 1 person in front of us, so we waited may be 2 or 3 minutes. When it was our turn, the lady asked, if it was our first time in Pan Pacific. When I said no, she looked us up in the computer and went in the back office and came back with 2 other desk clerks to assist others waiting to be checked in. She printed our check in form and room keys and said I will personally take you to your room. She grabbed my wife's bags and took us to our room on the 15th floor. She gave us her business card and told us to call her if we needed anything or a tour of the facilities including the club floor. We thought this was a great jesture, especially since the lobby was busy. Room was large, very clean, very well furnished. Bathroom is big with seperate tub and shower. Tub was deep but a bit short for my 5'11 body. Last time when we stayed (August 2004) they had wired internet. Now it is wireless. Internet speed was great and they charge SGD 26.50 a day.There are plenty of restaurants and shops in the area. Bus and Metra are close by, but we used taxis to get around. Taxis are always lined up in front of the hotel, and the bell staff will open the door for your taxi everytime.We have stayed at many hotels in Singapore, and this hotel is our favourite. I strongly recommend this hotel to anyone.
